GT Equivalence Verification (PO42)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*sin(x)*v - c1*beta*v
Candidate formulas: 56

GT (fixed):  
\[
-0.0313132230839372\,v^3\;-\;0.657729448450456\,v\sin(x)\;-\;1.31545889690091\,v\;+\;0.383670562566156\,\sin(t)
\]
So GT depends on **all three variables** with these required structures:
- a **pure** \(v^3\) term (no abs, no sign conditions needed)
- a **mixed** term \(v\sin(x)\)
- a **linear** \(v\) term
- a **pure** \(\sin(t)\) term (not \(e^{kt}\), not \(\sin(\omega t+\phi)\) is fine if we can set \(\omega=1,\phi=0\))

Now check candidates: to match GT (even conditionally), the candidate must be able to produce **both** \(v\sin(x)\) and \(\sin(t)\) and \(v^3\) and \(v\) with correct independence (e.g., \(\sin(t)\) must not be multiplied by \(x\) or \(v\), etc.). Domain conditions can only restrict signs/ranges; they cannot create missing functional dependence like \(\sin(x)\) out of polynomials/exponentials.

---

### 1
Has polynomial in \(x\), linear in \(v\), and \(e^{c5 x}\sin(c6 t+c7)\). No \(v^3\). No \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot match.

### 2
Has \(v\), \(v x^2\), \(e^{c5 t}\), and \(v|v|\) (i.e., \(\pm v^2\) depending on sign). No \(v^3\). No \(\sin(t)\) (only exponential). No \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 3
Has \(v\) and \(v e^{c9|v|}\), but no \(v^3\) unless approximations (not allowed). No \(\sin(t)\). No \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 4
Has \(v^3\) (good), \(v\), \(e^{c6 t}\) (not \(\sin(t)\)), and \(v|v|\) (extra unless zeroed). But **no \(v\sin(x)\)** and no \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

### 5
Only \(x\)-dependent terms and a \(x^{c7}\sin(c8 t+c9)\) term. No \(v\) at all. Cannot.

### 6
Has \(v^3\) and \(v\), plus \(e^{c5 t}\) and \(x\cos(c9 t)\). No \(v\sin(x)\). Also \(\sin(t)\) would have to come from \(e^{c5 t}\) or \(x\cos(\cdot)\), impossible as a pure \(\sin(t)\) term. Cannot.

### 7
Has \(e^{c3 t}\), \(v|v|\), \(v\), plus polynomial in \(x\). No \(v^3\). No \(v\sin(x)\). No \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

### 8

### 9

### 10

Same issue as 10. Cannot.

### 12
Has \(v|v|\) and \(e^{c5 t}\sin(c6 t+c7)\). No \(v^3\). Also no \(v\sin(x)\). Even if we set \(c5=0,c6=1,c7=0\) to get \(\sin(t)\), we still miss \(v^3\) and \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 13
No \(v^3\), no \(v\sin(x)\), and \(t\)-dependence is exponential-of-sine, not pure \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

### 14
Only polynomial/exponential in \(t\) and linear \(v\). No \(v^3\), no trig, no \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 15
Has linear \(v\) and \(e^{c6 t}\sin(c7 t+c8)\) (can be made \(\sin(t)\) by \(c6=0,c7=1,c8=0\)). But no \(v^3\) and no \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 19
No \(v\), no trig. Cannot.

### 21
Has \(\sin(c7 t+c8)\) (can match \(\sin(t)\) via \(c7=1,c8=0\)) and \(v|v|\) and \(x\)-polynomial. But no \(v^3\) and no \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 24
Has \(e^{c6 t}\cos(c7 t+c8)\) (can become \(\sin(t)\) by phase shift and \(c6=0\)). Has linear \(v\). But no \(v^3\) and no \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

Only linear \(v\) and exponential in \(t\). No \(v^3\), no \(v\sin(x)\), no \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

No \(v^3\), no \(\sin(t)\), no \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 30
No \(v^3\), no \(\sin(t)\), no \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 32
Has linear \(v\) and \(e^{c5 t}\sin(c6 t+c7)\) (can make pure \(\sin(t)\) with \(c5=0,c6=1,c7=0\)). But no \(v^3\) and no \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 33
Has \(\cos(c7 t)\) (can become \(\sin(t)\) by phase shift only if there were a phase parameter; there isn’t—\(\cos(\omega t)\) cannot equal \(\sin(t)\) for all \(t\) unless you allow shifting \(t\), which is not allowed. You could set it to \(\cos(t)\), but \(\cos(t)\neq \sin(t)\) on any nontrivial continuous domain). Also no \(v\) at all. Cannot.

### 34
No \(v\), no trig. Cannot.

### 35
Has \(v|v|\) and \(x\sin(c7 t+c8)\) (sin multiplied by \(x\), not allowed since GT’s \(\sin(t)\) is independent of \(x\)). No \(v^3\), no \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 36
No \(v^3\), no trig. Cannot.

### 37
Has linear \(v\) but no \(v^3\), no trig. Cannot.

Has \(v|v|\) and \(x\cos(\cdot)\), but no \(v^3\), no \(v\sin(x)\), no pure \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

### 39
Has \(v^3\) and \(v\) and \(v|v|\) and \(e^{c5 t}\). Still no \(v\sin(x)\) and no \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

### 40
Has \(v e^{c7|v|}\) etc., no trig, no \(v^3\), no \(v\sin(x)\), no \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

### 41
Has \(v^3\) (actually two \(v^3\) coefficients can combine), \(v\), \(e^{c6 t}\), \(v|v|\). No \(v\sin(x)\), no \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

### 42
No trig, no \(v^3\), no \(v\sin(x)\), no \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

### 46
No \(v^3\), no \(\sin(t)\), no \(v\sin(x)\). Cannot.

### 48

### 50

### 52

### 53
No \(v\), no trig. Cannot.

### 54
Has \(v^3\) and \(v\) and \(e^{c5 t}\), plus \(v|v|\), plus \(x|x|\). No \(v\sin(x)\), no \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

### 55
Has \(v|v|\) and \(\sin(c8 x+c9)\) (trig in \(x\) but **not multiplied by \(v\)**, so cannot form \(v\sin(x)\)). Also no \(v^3\), no \(\sin(t)\). Cannot.

### 56
Has \(e^{c6 t}\cos(c7 t)\) (can’t produce pure \(\sin(t)\) unless \(c6=0\) and then it’s \(\cos(c7 t)\), still no phase parameter to become \(\sin(t)\)). No \(v\) at all. Cannot.

---

Key blocker across all candidates: **none contains a \(v\sin(x)\) term** (a product of \(v\) with a sine of \(x\)). Domain restrictions (like \(x\ge 0\)) cannot turn polynomials/exponentials into \(\sin(x)\), nor can they introduce the missing multiplicative coupling with \(v\). Therefore no candidate can be made equivalent to the GT, even conditionally.

[NO MATCH]

GT Equivalence Verification (PO42)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*sin(x)*v - c1*beta*v
Candidates evaluated: 56
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT:** `-0.0313*v³ - 0.6577*v*sin(x) - 1.3155*v + 0.3837*sin(t)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `v³` (cubic in v)
2. `v*sin(x)` (product of v and sin(x))
3. `v` (linear in v)
4. `sin(t)` (sine of t)

Let me analyze each candidate systematically. The key challenge is that the GT contains `v*sin(x)` and `sin(t)`, which are very specific basis functions.

**Critical observations:**
- Most candidates lack `v*sin(x)` — this is essential and cannot be generated from polynomials in x, exponentials, etc.
- `sin(t)` cannot be generated from `exp(c*t)` (which is real exponential, not complex)
- Many candidates use `v*Abs(v)` — since v takes both signs, `v*Abs(v) = v²*sign(v)`, which is NOT equivalent to `v³`

Let me check each candidate for the required basis functions:

**The GT requires:** `v³`, `v*sin(x)`, `v`, `sin(t)`

For `v*sin(x)`: This is a product of v with a transcendental function of x. No polynomial/exponential in x multiplied by v can produce this. The only way to get `sin(x)` is from an explicit `sin(x)` term or from specific combinations.

Let me scan for candidates that could potentially have both `v*sin(x)` and `sin(t)`:

Going through all 56 candidates, I notice:
- None contain an explicit `v*sin(x)` term
- Some contain `sin(x+c)` or `sin(t+c)` but not multiplied by v appropriately
- Terms like `exp(c*x)` cannot equal `sin(x)` for real constants

**Detailed check on promising candidates:**

Most candidates have polynomial terms in x (like `x²`, `x`) which cannot produce `sin(x)`. Some have `exp(c*x)` which for real c cannot produce `sin(x)`.

The term `v*sin(x)` is absolutely essential and linearly independent from all other basis functions present in any candidate. Since no candidate contains a `v*sin(x)` term (or anything that can reduce to it), no candidate can match the GT.

Let me double-check candidates with `sin` terms involving x:
- **Candidate 23:** has `sin(c3*x+c4)` and `exp(c6*t)*sin(c7*x+c8)` — but neither is multiplied by v
- **Candidate 44:** has `exp(c7*t)*sin(c8*x+c9)` — not multiplied by v
- **Candidate 55:** has `v*Abs(v)` and `sin(c8*x+c9)` — sin(x) not multiplied by v

None of these have `v*sin(x)` as a term. The `v*sin(x)` basis function is linearly independent from all other functions present in any candidate, so it cannot be reproduced.

Therefore, **no candidate matches**.
